href="#ViewPollResults" onclick="if (!window.__cfRLUnblockHandlers) return false; poll_result(1); return false;" title="View Results Of This Poll" data-cf-modified-6973d2918b2fe47c567a94dd-="">View Results</a></p></div> </form></div> </div> </div> <div class="clearline"></div> </div> <div id="accordion"> <h2 class="accordion-toggle">About SGX Nifty <i class="fa fa-angle-double-right"></i> </h2> <div class="accordion-content"> <div class="entry-text"> <ul id="home-faq"><li><i class="grey"><b>What is <strong>SGX Nifty<br/></strong></b></i>SGX is one of the leading stock exchanges in Asia, movement on which somehow reflects in other stock indices in the continent.<strong>SGX Nifty</strong> is Singapore Stock Exchange Nifty, which implies the Indian CNX Nifty traded in Singapore exchange.It is a very popular derivative product of Singapore Exchange as it allows foreign investors to take a position in Indian Market.In Singapore Exchange, Indian stocks cannot be traded but it allows future products like <strong>SGX Nifty Futures</strong>. Thus, it is the derivative product of Singapore Exchange facilitating futures trading of underlying NSE Nifty index. It allows FII&#8217;s and other individuals to invest in Nifty Futures.</li><li><i class="grey"><b>What is the SGX Nifty Opening time?<br/></b></i>Since trading is done for NSE Index, Singapore Nifty is settled on the basis of the closing price of NSE Index price (S&amp;P CNX Nifty). Trading Timings &#8211; There are two types of Contracts in SGX with different settlement periods -1- E &#8211; SGX QUEST (T) Settlement same day, Timings- Mon-Fri &#8211; 9:00 am &#8211; 6:15 pm (6:30 am &#8211; 3:45 pm IST)<br/>2- E* &#8211; SGX QUEST (T+1) Settlement next day, Timings- Mon-Fri &#8211; 7:15 pm &#8211; 1:00 am (4:45 pm &#8211; 10:30 pm IST)These two contracts have different trading timings which enable traders all over the world to trade in SGX even if the market is closed. FII&#8217;s invest in Indian future contracts through SGX Nifty and India is 2.5 hours behind Singapore. SGX opens at 9:00 AM in Singapore i.e. 6:30 AM as per IST (Indian Standard Time).</li><li><i class="grey"><b><b>How does SGX Nifty work?<br/></b></b></i>By tracking Singapore Nifty, we can predict the initial direction of Indian Stock market.Singapore market opens around 2 hours before Indian market and directly relates to NSE market.It moves with respect to the Indian Nifty and hence can be used as a tool to predict the Indian market providing initial direction to the Indian market. Moreover, both India and Singapore fall in the same continent, which co-related both the markets and one most often decides the sentiments of the other market. This also makes it easy for Indian advisory and financial institutions to give trading recommendations on <strong>Nifty</strong> before opening.</li><li><i class="grey"><b><b>Can SGX Nifty help in my trading?<br/></b></b></i>Very first thing in the morning any Indian trader does is getting news on <strong>SGX Nifty Live</strong> on Singapore stock exchange, which trades before opening of Indian market . At what level <strong>SGX Nifty Live</strong> is trading will gives an indication of what will be the probable trend in Indian stock market when they will open for trading.The second thing would be listening on TV to technical analysts views on Nifty intraday and checking with financial advisors over a phone or through online or by way of SMS alerts.This whole thing sums up how crucial Nifty movement is for Indian markets. Technical analysis is perhaps the only logical way to find an answer to which direction Nifty will be moving in current market situation.</li><li><i class="grey"><b><b>How can I trade in Indian Stock Market?<br/></b></b></i>Trading in the Indian stock market is no longer a complicated task; thanks to the online phenomenon and IT conveniences. Both the NSE and BSE, the main index of the Indian market, have adopted the latest technology for smooth operations, also facilitating investors to trade online. At one time BSE and NSE trading was not all investors&#8217; cup of tea. Physical presence, lots of paperwork, lack of live market news, <strong>Live SGX Nifty</strong> News etc. attracted few investors. With the online trend incorporated, BSE and NSE trading became an effortless affair.The NSE and BSE market have already been attracting foreign investors. It is not only foreign investors but also domestic investors who can look forward towards seeing their money multiply from many NSE and BSE stock. Before you put in your money, do conduct a market research and stay updated with market news so that whatever stock you choose no matter whether it is NSE or BSE stock, turns out to be lucrative for you.With brokerage portals providing solutions to investors online, more and more investors are attracted towards BSE and NSE trading. All you need to do is get registered at the platform and start availing services. Choose only a reputed brokerage solutions provider, one that offers solutions beyond brokerage.</li><li><i class="grey"><b><b>What are other names used for SGX Nifty?<br/></b></b></i>Some of the names / alias used for SGX Nifty are <strong>SGX Singapore Nifty, </strong><strong>Singapore Nifty, </strong><strong>Sgx Nifty Futures,</strong><strong>Singapore Nifty Futures, </strong><strong>SGX Aftermarket Future, </strong><strong>Sgx Nifty Live, </strong><strong>Sgx Nifty Future</strong></li></ul> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </article> </div> <div id="comment-jump" class="comments"> </div> <div class="clearline"></div> </div> <div class="clear"></div> <div class="ads mb10"><div id="ad_bottom_sticky"><script type="6973d2918b2fe47c567a94dd-text/javascript">googletag.cmd.push(function(){googletag.display("ad_bottom_sticky")})</script></div><script type="6973d2918b2fe47c567a94dd-text/javascript" language="javascript" src="https://live.primis.tech/live/liveView.php?s=119775"></script></div> <div class="clearline mb10"></div> <div id="reload_box" class="reload_box"> <form method="post" id="reload_form"> <input class="field reload_minute" type="number" min="0" max="60" onkeydown="if (!window.__cfRLUnblockHandlers) return false; if (event.keyCode == 13) document.getElementById('reload_button').click()" id="reload_minute" name="reload_minute" data-cf-modified-6973d2918b2fe47c567a94dd-=""> <button id="reload_button" class="button reload_button" onclick="if (!window.__cfRLUnblockHandlers) return false; reload_set_cookie('reload_minute', 'reload_minute')" type="submit" data-cf-modified-6973d2918b2fe47c567a94dd-="">Set Reload Minutes</button> </form> <p id="demo"></p> <div class="reload_text">Set Reload Time in Minutes.
